<script>;(function() {

'use strict';


window.TSMark = function(mark_label) {
	if (!window.performance || !window.performance.mark) return;
	performance.mark(mark_label);
};
window.TSMark('start_load');


window.TSMeasureAndBeacon = function(measure_label, start_mark_label) {
	if (start_mark_label === 'start_nav' && window.performance && window.performance.timing) {
		window.TSBeacon(measure_label, (new Date()).getTime() - performance.timing.navigationStart);
		return;
	}
	if (!window.performance || !window.performance.mark || !window.performance.measure) return;
	performance.mark(start_mark_label + '_end');
	try {
		performance.measure(measure_label, start_mark_label, start_mark_label + '_end');
		window.TSBeacon(measure_label, performance.getEntriesByName(measure_label)[0].duration);
	} catch(e) { return; }
};


if ('sendBeacon' in navigator) {
	window.TSBeacon = function(label, value) {
		var endpoint_url = window.ts_endpoint_url || 'https://slack.com/beacon/timing';
		navigator.sendBeacon(endpoint_url + '?data=' + encodeURIComponent(label + ':' + value), '');
	};
} else {
	window.TSBeacon = function(label, value) {
		var endpoint_url = window.ts_endpoint_url || 'https://slack.com/beacon/timing';
		(new Image()).src = endpoint_url + '?data=' + encodeURIComponent(label + ':' + value);
	};
}

})();
</script>

<script>(function() {
        'use strict';

        window.callSlackAPIUnauthed = function(method, args, callback) {
                var timestamp = Date.now() / 1000;  
                var version = (window.TS && TS.boot_data) ? TS.boot_data.version_uid.substring(0, 8) : 'noversion';
                var url = '/api/' + method + '?_x_id=' + version + '-' + timestamp;
                var req = new XMLHttpRequest();

                req.onreadystatechange = function() {
                        if (req.readyState == 4) {
                                req.onreadystatechange = null;
                                var obj;

                                if (req.status == 200 || req.status == 429) {
                                        try {
                                                obj = JSON.parse(req.responseText);
                                        } catch (err) {
                                                console.warn('unable to do anything with api rsp');
                                        }
                                }

                                obj = obj || {
                                        ok: false
                                }

                                callback(obj.ok, obj, args);
                        }
                }

                var async = true;
                req.open('POST', url, async);

                var form_data = new FormData();
                var has_data = false;
                Object.keys(args).map(function(k) {
                        if (k[0] === '_') return;
                        form_data.append(k, args[k]);
                        has_data = true;
                });

                if (has_data) {
                        req.send(form_data);
                } else {
                        req.send();
                }
        }
})();</script>

	<script type="text/javascript">



var TS_last_log_date = null;
var TSMakeLogDate = function() {
	var date = new Date();

	var y = date.getFullYear();
	var mo = date.getMonth()+1;
	var d = date.getDate();

	var time = {
	  h: date.getHours(),
	  mi: date.getMinutes(),
	  s: date.getSeconds(),
	  ms: date.getMilliseconds()
	};

	Object.keys(time).map(function(moment, index) {
		if (moment == 'ms') {
			if (time[moment] < 10) {
				time[moment] = time[moment]+'00';
			} else if (time[moment] < 100) {
				time[moment] = time[moment]+'0';
			}
		} else if (time[moment] < 10) {
			time[moment] = '0' + time[moment];
		}
	});

	var str = y + '/' + mo + '/' + d + ' ' + time.h + ':' + time.mi + ':' + time.s + '.' + time.ms;
	if (TS_last_log_date) {
		var diff = date-TS_last_log_date;
		//str+= ' ('+diff+'ms)';
	}
	TS_last_log_date = date;
	return str+' ';
}

var parseDeepLinkRequest = function(code) {
	var m = code.match(/"id":"([CDG][A-Z0-9]{8})"/);
	var id = m ? m[1] : null;

	m = code.match(/"team":"(T[A-Z0-9]{8})"/);
	var team = m ? m[1] : null;

	m = code.match(/"message":"([0-9]+\.[0-9]+)"/);
	var message = m ? m[1] : null;

	return { id: id, team: team, message: message };
}

if ('rendererEvalAsync' in window) {
	var origRendererEvalAsync = window.rendererEvalAsync;
	window.rendererEvalAsync = function(blob) {
		try {
			var data = JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(atob(blob)));
			if (data.code.match(/handleDeepLink/)) {
				var request = parseDeepLinkRequest(data.code);
				if (!request.id || !request.team || !request.message) return;

				request.cmd = 'channel';
				TSSSB.handleDeepLinkWithArgs(JSON.stringify(request));
				return;
			} else {
				origRendererEvalAsync(blob);
			}
		} catch (e) {
		}
	}
}
</script>

<script>TSSSB.env = (function() {
	'use strict';

	var v = {
		win_ssb_version: null,
		win_ssb_version_minor: null,
		mac_ssb_version: null,
		mac_ssb_version_minor: null,
		mac_ssb_build: null,
		lin_ssb_version: null,
		lin_ssb_version_minor: null,
		desktop_app_version: null
	};

	var is_win = (navigator.appVersion.indexOf("Windows") !== -1);
	var is_lin = (navigator.appVersion.indexOf("Linux") !== -1);
	var is_mac = !!(navigator.userAgent.match(/(OS X)/g));

	if (navigator.userAgent.match(/(Slack_SSB)/g) || navigator.userAgent.match(/(Slack_WINSSB)/g)) {
		
		var parts = navigator.userAgent.split('/');
		var version_str = parts[parts.length-1];
		var version_float = parseFloat(version_str);
		var version_parts = version_str.split('.');
		var version_minor = (version_parts.length == 3) ? parseInt(version_parts[2]) : 0;

		if (navigator.userAgent.match(/(AtomShell)/g)) {
			
			if (is_lin) {
				v.lin_ssb_version = version_float;
				v.lin_ssb_version_minor = version_minor;
			} else if (is_win) {
				v.win_ssb_version = version_float;
				v.win_ssb_version_minor = version_minor;
			} else if (is_mac) {
				v.mac_ssb_version = version_float;
				v.mac_ssb_version_minor = version_minor;
			}

			if (version_parts.length >= 3) {
				v.desktop_app_version = {
					major: parseInt(version_parts[0]),
					minor: parseInt(version_parts[1]),
					patch: parseInt(version_parts[2])
				}
			}
		} else {
			
			v.mac_ssb_version = version_float;
			v.mac_ssb_version_minor = version_minor;

			
			
			var app_ver = window.macgap && macgap.app && macgap.app.buildVersion && macgap.app.buildVersion();
			var matches = String(app_ver).match(/(?:\()(.*)(?:\))/);
			v.mac_ssb_build = (matches && matches.length == 2) ? parseInt(matches[1] || 0) : 0;
		}
	}

	return v;
})();
</script>

		&lt;link&gt;https://wordpress-freemansmith.c9users.io/gore-drug/?page_id=2&lt;/link&gt;

		&lt;description&gt;&lt;/description&gt;
		&lt;content:encoded&gt;&lt;![CDATA[This is an example page. It&#039;s different from a blog post because it will stay in one place and will show up in your site navigation (in most themes). Most people start with an About page that introduces them to potential site visitors. It might say something like this:

&lt;blockquote&gt;Hi there! I&#039;m a bike messenger by day, aspiring actor by night, and this is my website. I live in Los Angeles, have a great dog named Jack, and I like pi&amp;#241;a coladas. (And gettin&#039; caught in the rain.)&lt;/blockquote&gt;

...or something like this:

&lt;blockquote&gt;The XYZ Doohickey Company was founded in 1971, and has been providing quality doohickeys to the public ever since. Located in Gotham City, XYZ employs over 2,000 people and does all kinds of awesome things for the Gotham community.&lt;/blockquote&gt;

As a new WordPress user, you should go to &lt;a href=&quot;https://wordpress-drakkensaer.c9users.io/gore-drug/wp-admin/&quot;&gt;your dashboard&lt;/a&gt; to delete this page and create new pages for your content. Have fun!]]&gt;&lt;/content:encoded&gt;

		&lt;title&gt;About&lt;/title&gt;
		&lt;link&gt;https://wordpress-freemansmith.c9users.io/gore-drug/?page_id=51&lt;/link&gt;
		&lt;pubDate&gt;Fri, 05 Feb 2016 18:53:28 +0000&lt;/pubDate&gt;
		&lt;dc:creator&gt;&lt;![CDATA[InboundRx]]&gt;&lt;/dc:creator&gt;

		&lt;wp:post_id&gt;51&lt;/wp:post_id&gt;
		&lt;wp:post_date&gt;&lt;![CDATA[2016-02-05 18:53:28]]&gt;&lt;/wp:post_date&gt;
		&lt;wp:post_date_gmt&gt;&lt;![CDATA[2016-02-05 18:53:28]]&gt;&lt;/wp:post_date_gmt&gt;

		&lt;wp:ping_status&gt;&lt;![CDATA[closed]]&gt;&lt;/wp:ping_status&gt;
		&lt;wp:post_name&gt;&lt;![CDATA[about]]&gt;&lt;/wp:post_name&gt;

			&lt;wp:meta_key&gt;&lt;![CDATA[_edit_last]]&gt;&lt;/wp:meta_key&gt;
			&lt;wp:meta_value&gt;&lt;![CDATA[1]]&gt;&lt;/wp:meta_value&gt;

			&lt;wp:meta_key&gt;&lt;![CDATA[_wp_page_template]]&gt;&lt;/wp:meta_key&gt;
			&lt;wp:meta_value&gt;&lt;![CDATA[subpage-about.php]]&gt;&lt;/wp:meta_value&gt;
		&lt;/wp:postmeta&gt;
		&lt;wp:postmeta&gt;
			&lt;wp:meta_key&gt;&lt;![CDATA[title]]&gt;&lt;/wp:meta_key&gt;
			&lt;wp:meta_value&gt;&lt;![CDATA[Family owned, independent pharmacies committed to our communities since 1957.]]&gt;&lt;/wp:meta_value&gt;
		&lt;/wp:postmeta&gt;
		&lt;wp:postmeta&gt;
			&lt;wp:meta_key&gt;&lt;![CDATA[_title]]&gt;&lt;/wp:meta_key&gt;
			&lt;wp:meta_value&gt;&lt;![CDATA[field_56b4d80a0db42]]&gt;&lt;/wp:meta_value&gt;
		&lt;/wp:postmeta&gt;
		&lt;wp:postmeta&gt;
			&lt;wp:meta_key&gt;&lt;![CDATA[content]]&gt;&lt;/wp:meta_key&gt;
			&lt;wp:meta_value&gt;&lt;![CDATA[The US Navy and World War II brought together Walter Haller and Lenna Belle Flannery at the Naval Air Station in Alameda. They were married in Seattle. Shortly after the war, through Belles encouragement, Walter attended the UC Medical School of Pharmacy. With Belles experience in pharmacy and now Walters degree, they opened their first store in Newark, CA. Shortly after, they were invited to purchase a second pharmacy, opening on March 18, 1957.

The Hallers Pharmacies were dedicated to the needs of the community from the start: holidays hours, open late night for local doctors to fill prescriptions, even the first in the area to offer medical supplies like crutches and wheelchairs.

Growing to 4 stores in the Newark / Fremont area, through almost 20 years of the Hallers hard work, 14 hours a day, 7 days a week they finally hung their hats and sold the business in 1975. Their legacy of independence and professionalism continues to this day through their now 10 stores branching to serve Fremont, Gilroy, Salinas and Walnut Creek.
&lt;div id=&quot;about-obit&quot;&gt;

&lt;img class=&quot;aligncenter size-full wp-image-131&quot; src=&quot;/wp-content/uploads/sites/4/2016/02/wmhaller.jpg&quot; alt=&quot;Walter Haller&#039;s Obituary&quot; width=&quot;200&quot; height=&quot;246&quot; /&gt;
&lt;h4&gt;Walter Martin Haller
May 30, 1919  Jan. 28, 2016&lt;/h4&gt;
Hallers Pharmacy founder dies peacefully at 96.

Following a private service in Oakdale, CA on February 3, 2016, Walter was buried alongside his wife of more than 62 years, Lena Belle, who preceded him in death in 2004.

He is survived by daughters Mary Louise Haller and Doris Jeanne Condren, son-in-law John Condren, seven grandchildren and six great grandchildren, along with his community friends of Morgan Hill, CA.

The family extends its gratitude to those customers who made it possible for Hallers to thrive as a family-owned pharmacy since 1957 and who brought joy to Walter and Belle as they worked behind the counter and made prescription deliveries.

Special thanks to all the members of Valley Pines Assisted Living and Vitas Hospice Care in Morgan Hill, CA.

In Walters memory, we frequently remember his words: When families brought their babies in, so I could see them, I knew we had made a good connection in the community.

&lt;/div&gt;]]&gt;&lt;/wp:meta_value&gt;

As a comprehensive service, Hallers Medication Concierge Program helps physicians meet the requirements of the new performance-based rating system while offering a convenient service to their patients through our stores.]]&gt;&lt;/wp:meta_value&gt;

		&lt;wp:postmeta&gt;
			&lt;wp:meta_key&gt;&lt;![CDATA[_lyt_0_button]]&gt;&lt;/wp:meta_key&gt;
			&lt;wp:meta_value&gt;&lt;![CDATA[field_56b5004249ff5]]&gt;&lt;/wp:meta_value&gt;
		&lt;/wp:postmeta&gt;
		&lt;wp:postmeta&gt;
			&lt;wp:meta_key&gt;&lt;![CDATA[lyt_0_content]]&gt;&lt;/wp:meta_key&gt;
			&lt;wp:meta_value&gt;&lt;![CDATA[&lt;strong&gt;The Concierge Program for Physicians&lt;/strong&gt;

&lt;em&gt;Step One: Lets Plan Together&lt;/em&gt;

Our pharmacy specialist will discuss with you the compliance and adherence of the patients already refilling your prescribed medications in our pharmacies. Through granular data, charts and tables you will be able to see the progress of each patient through their medication history.

&lt;em&gt;Step Two: We help you enroll more patients&lt;/em&gt;

Our pharmacy specialist will then show you the process in which a patient can enroll into the system. We will provide you with all the literature, samples and instructions, free of charge.

&lt;em&gt;Step Three: Track and Adjust&lt;/em&gt;

Every three months we will analyze your Physician Performance Star Rating, identify specific conditions in which patients struggle with their medications and how we can work together to improve your performance, patients adherence and compliance.

&lt;strong&gt;The Concierge Program for Patients&lt;/strong&gt;

Once your patients are enrolled in the Concierge Program, Hallers Pharmacy works with them directly through personalized, customized options to make it easy for anyone to stay compliant and adherent:

&lt;em&gt;Medication Synchronization.&lt;/em&gt; We will analyze and determine the best time period in which your patient can pick up all of their medications in one single day, reducing multiple trips to the pharmacy.

&lt;em&gt;Advanced Medication Packing. &lt;/em&gt;We offer state of the art technology to offer your patient convenient ways of taking their medications at home and on the go.
&lt;p style=&quot;padding-left: 30px;&quot;&gt;Vials. Latest vial technology for oral solids, liquids and ointments containers.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p style=&quot;padding-left: 30px;&quot;&gt;Multi-Dose Blister Packs. Helps your patients know all the medications they need to take at specific times and specific days by just punching the blister, simplifying knowing the medication was taken and when.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p style=&quot;padding-left: 30px;&quot;&gt;Strip Packaging. Makes it easy for mobile patients to take their medications with them. Organized by day and time, each package is firmly sealed, clearly labeled and easy to open.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;em&gt;Medication Pickup or Delivery.&lt;/em&gt; With 10 pharmacies in the San Jose / San Francisco area, we offer in-store pickup, home / facility delivery and mail order prescription fulfillment.

&lt;em&gt;Medication Therapy Management, MTM.&lt;/em&gt; Our pharmacist will discuss directly with your patients their current medication regime, issues preventing the patient to adhere to the regime, issues with the formulation, drug interactions and any other issue that may prevent a patient from receiving the best possible care through medication.]]&gt;&lt;/wp:meta_value&gt;

		var g_editor;

		$(function(){

			var wrap_long_lines = !!TS.model.code_wrap_long_lines;

			g_editor = CodeMirror(function(elt){
				var content = document.getElementById("file_contents");
				content.parentNode.replaceChild(elt, content);
			}, {
				value: $('#file_contents').text(),
				lineNumbers: true,
				matchBrackets: true,
				indentUnit: 4,
				indentWithTabs: true,
				enterMode: "keep",
				tabMode: "shift",
				viewportMargin: 10,
				readOnly: true,
				lineWrapping: wrap_long_lines
			});

			// past a certain point, CodeMirror rendering may simply stop working.
			// start having CodeMirror use its Long List View-style scolling at >= max_lines.
			var max_lines = 8192;

			var snippet_lines;

			// determine # of lines, limit height accordingly
			if (g_editor.doc && g_editor.doc.lineCount) {
				snippet_lines = parseInt(g_editor.doc.lineCount());
				var new_height;
				if (snippet_lines) {
					// we want the CodeMirror container to collapse around short snippets.
					// however, we want to let it auto-expand only up to a limit, at which point
					// we specify a fixed height so CM can display huge snippets without dying.
					// this is because CodeMirror works nicely with no height set, but doesn't
					// scale (big file performance issue), and doesn't work with min/max-height -
					// so at some point, we have to set an absolute height to kick it into its
					// smart / partial "Long List View"-style rendering mode.
					if (snippet_lines < max_lines) {
						new_height = 'auto';
					} else {
						new_height = (max_lines * 0.875) + 'rem'; // line-to-rem ratio
					}
					var line_count = Math.min(snippet_lines, max_lines);
					TS.info('Applying height of ' + new_height + ' to container for this snippet of ' + snippet_lines + (snippet_lines === 1 ? ' line' : ' lines'));
					$('#page .CodeMirror').height(new_height);
				}
			}

			$('#file_preview_wrap_cb').bind('change', function(e) {
				TS.model.code_wrap_long_lines = $(this).prop('checked');
				g_editor.setOption('lineWrapping', TS.model.code_wrap_long_lines);
			})

			$('#file_preview_wrap_cb').prop('checked', wrap_long_lines);

			CodeMirror.switchSlackMode(g_editor, "xml");
		});
